--drop database if exists avonehr;
--create database avonehr;
--use avonehr;


--our clients, also known as doctors or physicians
drop table if exists client cascade;
create table client (
  id serial primary key,
  name varchar(255),
  code varchar(100),
  address varchar(100),
  address2 varchar(100),
  city varchar(50),
  state varchar(2),
  postal varchar(10), --zipcode
  country varchar(2),
  phone varchar(50),
  fax varchar(50),
  email varchar(50),
  website varchar(50), --url
  calendar_start_time time,
  calendar_end_time time,
  functional_range boolean,     --if client wants to use functional ranges in addition to conventional ranges for lab test results
  ein varchar(50),
  npi varchar(50),
  labcorp_api_key varchar(100),
  quest_api_key varchar(100),
  doctors_data_username varchar(100),
  doctors_data_password varchar(100),
  stripe_api_key varchar(200),
  bluefin_api_key varchar(100),
  specialty_lab_ordering boolean, --default false  #if true then we will order labs for patients and charge an extra fee.
  note varchar(1000),
  created TIMESTAMP WITHOUT TIME ZONE,
  created_user_id int,
  updated TIMESTAMP WITHOUT TIME ZONE,
  updated_user_id int
);

create unique index client_name on client (name);
create unique index code_name on client (code);
create unique index phone_name on client (phone);
create unique index fax_name on client (fax);
create unique index email_name on client (email);
create unique index website_name on client (website);
create unique index ein_name on client (ein);
create unique index npi_name on client (npi);

--record the patient page card positions
drop table if exists user_grid cascade;
create table user_grid (
user_id int primary key,
layout varchar(5000),
created TIMESTAMP WITHOUT TIME ZONE,
updated TIMESTAMP WITHOUT TIME ZONE
);


--users are the many employees of a doctors office
drop table if exists users cascade;
create table users (
  id serial primary key,
  client_id int,
  firstname varchar(255),
  lastname varchar(255),
  title varchar(255),
  email varchar(255),
  phone varchar(25),
  signature bytea,
  note varchar(1000),
  status char(1),    --A=Active, I=Inactive, D=Deleted
  appointments boolean,   --Determines if patients may make appointments with this user from the patient portal.
  type varchar(255),      --PP=Primary Provider, SP=Secondary Provider, A=Administrative, L=Limited
  schedule varchar(255),  --F=Full, H=Half, Q=Quarter
  admin boolean,
  password varchar(255),
  npi varchar(255),
  medical_license varchar(255),
  email_confirm_dt date,    --date confirmed email address
  token varchar(255), --new client setup
  reset_password_token varchar(255),
  reset_password_expires TIMESTAMP WITHOUT TIME ZONE,
  sign_dt TIMESTAMP WITHOUT TIME ZONE,   --date accepted terms and conditions with e-signature
  sign_ip_address varchar(20),  --IP address when signed terms and conditions with e-signature
  login_dt date,   --date last logged into site
  email_forward_user_id int,
  timezone char(4),
  created TIMESTAMP WITHOUT TIME ZONE,
  created_user_id int,
  updated TIMESTAMP WITHOUT TIME ZONE,
  updated_user_id int
);

create index on users using btree (client_id); --so client can select their list of users
create unique index email_client on client (email);

--the patients of the doctor
drop table if exists patient cascade;
create table patient (
  id serial primary key,
  client_id int,
  user_id int,  --which provider sees this patient
  status char(1),   --A=Active, I=Inactive, T=Trouble
  firstname varchar(30),
  middlename varchar(20),
  lastname varchar(30),
  preferred_name varchar(30),
  address varchar(100),
  address2 varchar(100),
  city varchar(50),
  state varchar(3), --country AU has a state with 3 characters
  postal varchar(10),
  country varchar(255),
  phone_home varchar(50),
  phone_cell varchar(50),
  phone_work varchar(50),
  phone_other varchar(50),
  phone_note varchar(50),
  email varchar(40),
  password varchar(255),
  dob date,
  ssn varchar(20),
  gender char(1), 
  emergency_firstname varchar(40),
  emergency_middlename varchar(40),
  emergency_lastname varchar(40),
  emergency_relationship varchar(40),
  emergency_email varchar(40),
  emergency_phone varchar(40),
  insurance_name varchar(50),
  insurance_group varchar(50),
  insurance_member varchar(50),
  insurance_phone varchar(50),
  insurance_desc varchar(50),
  login_dt date,    --date last logged into site
  primary_reason varchar(1000),
  admin_note text,
  medical_note text,
  referred_by varchar(100),
  height int,
  waist int,
  weight int,
  pharmacy_id int,  --fk to pharmacy.id
  pharmacy2_id int,   --fk to pharmacy.id 
  reset_password_token varchar(255),
  reset_password_expires TIMESTAMP WITHOUT TIME ZONE,
  signature varchar(100),
  stripe_customer_id varchar(45),
  corp_stripe_customer_id varchar(45),
  created TIMESTAMP WITHOUT TIME ZONE,
  created_user_id int,
  updated TIMESTAMP WITHOUT TIME ZONE,
  updated_user_id int
);

create index on patient using btree (client_id, firstname); 
create index on patient using btree (client_id, lastname); 
create index on patient using btree (client_id, phone_cell); 
create index on patient using btree (client_id, phone_home); 

create unique index email_patient on patient (client_id, email);	--one patients email can be used at several clients

drop table if exists contract cascade;
create table contract (
  id serial primary key, 
  contract varchar(10000),
  created TIMESTAMP WITHOUT TIME ZONE
);

drop table if exists user_contract cascade;
create table user_contract (
  id serial primary key, 
  client_id int,
  user_id int,
  contract_id int,
  filename varchar(100),
  created TIMESTAMP WITHOUT TIME ZONE
);


drop table if exists payment_method cascade;
create table payment_method (
  id serial primary key, 
  patient_id int,
  type char(2) check (type in ('C', 'CH')),  --C=Card, CH=Checking Account
  account_number varchar(4),
  exp varchar(10),
  address varchar(100),
  address2 varchar(100),
  city varchar(50),
  state varchar(2),
  postal varchar(10),   --zipcode
  country varchar(2),
  phone varchar(50),
  status char(1),   --D=Deleted
  stripe_payment_method_token varchar(45),
  corp_stripe_payment_method_token varchar(45),
  client_id int,
  created TIMESTAMP WITHOUT TIME ZONE,
  created_user_id int,
  updated TIMESTAMP WITHOUT TIME ZONE,
  updated_user_id int
);

insert into payment_method (patient_id, type, account_number, exp, address, address2, city, state, postal, country, phone, status, stripe_payment_method_token, corp_stripe_payment_method_token, client_id, created, created_user_id, updated, updated_user_id

--this stores a list of appointment types
drop table if exists appointment_type cascade;
create table appointment_type (
  id serial primary key,
  client_id int,
  appointment_type varchar(50),
  descr varchar(1000),
  length int,
  fee decimal(5,2),
  allow_patients_schedule boolean,
  sort_order int,
  active boolean,
  note varchar(200),
  created TIMESTAMP WITHOUT TIME ZONE,
  created_user_id int,
  updated TIMESTAMP WITHOUT TIME ZONE,
  updated_user_id int
);

create index on appointment_type using btree (client_id);

--this shows which users use which appointment types, this is a many to many table
drop table if exists appointment_type_user cascade;
create table appointment_type_user (
  client_id int,
  user_id int,
  appointment_type_id int,
  active boolean,
  amount int,
  created TIMESTAMP WITHOUT TIME ZONE,
  created_user_id int,
  updated TIMESTAMP WITHOUT TIME ZONE,
  updated_user_id int
);

alter table appointment_type_user add primary key (client_id, user_id, appointment_type_id);
create index on appointment_type_user using btree (appointment_type_id); --for delete

--this stores the list of clients forms, such as the registration form, symptom survey, etc
drop table if exists client_form cascade;
create table client_form (
  id serial primary key,
  client_id int,
  active boolean,
  type char(1),     --S=Signup form, which is the patient registration form that every client must have
  title varchar(255),
  form varchar(10000),
  notes varchar(100),
  created TIMESTAMP WITHOUT TIME ZONE,
  created_user_id int,
  updated TIMESTAMP WITHOUT TIME ZONE,
  updated_user_id int
);
create index on client_form using btree (client_id); --for delete 

insert into client_form (client_id,active,type,title,form,notes,created,created_user_id,updated,updated_user_id) values(1, true, 'S', 'Registration', '<form className={classes.form} noValidate>...', 'Notes', now(), 1, now(), 1);

--alter table client_form add foreign key (created_user_id) references user(id);
--alter table client_form add foreign key (updated_user_id) references user(id);


--labs are documents from laboratories
--see examples in /avonehr_spec/misc/lab_samples
drop table if exists lab cascade;
create table lab (
  id serial primary key,
  client_id int,
  user_id int,      --used during workflow to assign to a user
  patient_id int,
  filename varchar(255),
  lab_dt TIMESTAMP WITHOUT TIME ZONE,          --The lab date that was parsed
  physician varchar(255),   --The physician name that was parsed
  type char(1),     --L=Lab, I=Imaging, M=Misc
  note varchar(1000),
  note_assign varchar(1000),
  source char(1), --where the document came from, P=patient portal, U=user, L=lab company ie doctors data FTP etc, F=fax
  lab_company_id int, --fk to lab_company.id
  status char(1),   --R=Requested, A=Approved, D=Declined
  deleted_dt date,  --so the cron job to delete labs knows its been 30 days since deletion
  created TIMESTAMP WITHOUT TIME ZONE,
  created_user_id int,
  updated TIMESTAMP WITHOUT TIME ZONE,
  updated_user_id int
);

create index on lab using btree (client_id, patient_id);

--alter table lab add foreign key (patient_id) references patient(id);
--alter table lab add foreign key (created_user_id) references user(id);
--alter table lab add foreign key (updated_user_id) references user(id);
--alter table lab add foreign key (lab_company_id) references lab_company(id);


--New
drop table if exists lab_history cascade;
create table lab_history as select * from lab where false;
alter table lab_history add primary key (id, created);
insert into lab_history (id, client_id, user_id, created, created_user_id) values (1, 1, 1, '2020-01-01', 1);
insert into lab_history (id, client_id, user_id, created, created_user_id) values (1, 1, 2, '2020-02-01', 1);

--alter table lab_history add foreign key (id) references lab(id);
--alter table lab_history add foreign key (user_id) references user(id);
--alter table lab_history add foreign key (client_id) references client(id);
--alter table lab_history add foreign key (patient_id) references patient(id);
--alter table lab_history add foreign key (created_user_id) references user(id);
--alter table lab_history add foreign key (updated_user_id) references user(id);
--alter table lab_history add foreign key (lab_company_id) references lab_company(id);


drop table if exists proc cascade;
create table proc (
  id varchar(20) primary key,
  name varchar(100),
  client_id int,    --so a client can create their own code, primarily done to create their own set of labs in one group
  type char(1), --L=Lab, this is determined if Labcorp says it is a lab
  lab_company_id int,
  sample_type_id int,  --fk to sample_type.id
  phlebotomy boolean,
  msrp decimal(6,2),    --the higher price
  price decimal(6,2),   --the real price
  notes varchar(1000),
  url varchar(500),
  status char(1),    --Null=Active, I=Inactive, D=Deleted
  created TIMESTAMP WITHOUT TIME ZONE,
  created_user_id int,
  updated TIMESTAMP WITHOUT TIME ZONE,
  updated_user_id int
);

create index on proc using btree (client_id); 
create index on proc using btree (name); 

--alter table proc add index (type, name);  #client_range.png searches by type=L

--alter table proc add foreign key (client_id) references client(id);
--alter table proc add foreign key (lab_company_id) references lab_company(id);
--alter table proc add foreign key (sample_type_id) references sample_type(id);

  client_id int,
  icd_id varchar(10),
  favorite boolean,
  created TIMESTAMP WITHOUT TIME ZONE,
  created_user_id int,
  updated TIMESTAMP WITHOUT TIME ZONE,
  updated_user_id int
);

--the patients encounters
drop table if exists encounter cascade;
create table encounter (
  id serial primary key,
  client_id int,
  user_id int,
  patient_id int,
  dt TIMESTAMP WITHOUT TIME ZONE,
  type_id char(1),  --fk to encounter_type.id
  title varchar(200),
  notes varchar(5000),
  treatment varchar(5000),
  read_dt date,   --when patient views treatment plan in portal
  lab_bill_to char(1),  --P=Patient, D=Doctor, I=Insurance
  created TIMESTAMP WITHOUT TIME ZONE,
  created_user_id int,
  updated TIMESTAMP WITHOUT TIME ZONE,
  updated_user_id int
);
create index on encounter using btree (patient_id);  --to pull the list of encounters for that patient
create index on encounter using btree (user_id); --to pull by user

insert into encounter values(1, 1, 1, 1, '2020-01-01 10:00:00', 'O', 'Initial Consult', '', '', null, 'P', now(), 1, null, null);
select setval(pg_get_serial_sequence('encounter', 'id'), (select max(id) from encounter)); --fix primary key sequence

--alter table encounter add foreign key (client_id) references client(id);
--alter table encounter add foreign key (user_id) references user(id);
--alter table encounter add foreign key (patient_id) references patient(id);
--alter table encounter add foreign key (type_id) references encounter_type(id);
--alter table encounter add foreign key (created_user_id) references user(id);
--alter table encounter add foreign key (updated_user_id) references user(id);


--the ICD codes (disease diagnosis) assigned in an encounter
drop table if exists patient_icd cascade;
create table patient_icd (
  id serial primary key,
  patient_id int,
  icd_id varchar(10),
  is_primary boolean,
  active boolean,
  client_id int,
  user_id int,
  encounter_id int,
  created TIMESTAMP WITHOUT TIME ZONE,
  created_user_id int,
  updated TIMESTAMP WITHOUT TIME ZONE,
  updated_user_id int
);

create index on patient_icd using btree (patient_id); --encounter_assesment_hover.png user recent 
create index on patient_icd using btree (user_id, created); --encounter_assesment_hover.png user recent

--the drugs assigned in one encounter
drop table if exists patient_drug cascade;
create table patient_drug (
  id serial primary key,
  patient_id int,
  drug_id int,
  drug_strength_id int,
  drug_frequency_id char(2),
  start_dt date,
  expires int,
  amount int,
  refills int,
  generic boolean,
  patient_instructions varchar(500),
  pharmacy_instructions varchar(500),
  pharmacy_id int,  --fk to pharmacy.id
  encounter_id int,
  client_id int,
  user_id int,
  created TIMESTAMP WITHOUT TIME ZONE,
  created_user_id int,
  updated TIMESTAMP WITHOUT TIME ZONE,
  updated_user_id int
);

create index on patient_drug using btree (patient_id);
create index on patient_drug using btree (user_id, created); --for encounter_plan_drug.png user recent query

drop table if exists patient_proc cascade;
create table patient_proc (
  id serial primary key,
  patient_id int,
  proc_id varchar(10),
  tranc_id int,         --shows test was paid
  lab_order_received_dt date,   --date lab sent kit to patient
  lab_sample_received_dt date,  --date lab received kit back from patient
  lab_completed_dt date,    --shows we received test results from lab
  client_id int,
  encounter_id int,
  created TIMESTAMP WITHOUT TIME ZONE,
  created_user_id int,
  updated TIMESTAMP WITHOUT TIME ZONE,
  updated_user_id int
);

create index on patient_proc using btree (patient_id);
create index on patient_proc using btree (client_id, proc_id); --for delete

--sometimes on a lab order the doctor wants to remove some ICD codes so we track that here

create table patient_proc_exception_icd (
  encounter_id int,
  icd_id varchar(100),
  created TIMESTAMP WITHOUT TIME ZONE
);
alter table patient_proc_exception_icd add primary key (encounter_id, icd_id);

--this stores the forms that the patient fills out
drop table if exists patient_form cascade;
create table patient_form (
  patient_id int,   --fk to patient.id
  form_id int, --fk to client_form.id
  form varchar(10000), --this has the data entered in the form at client_form.form
  sign_dt TIMESTAMP WITHOUT TIME ZONE,
  sign_ip_address varchar(20),
  client_id int,
  created TIMESTAMP WITHOUT TIME ZONE
);
alter table patient_form add primary key (patient_id, form_id);

--alter table patient_form add foreign key (form_id) references client_form(id);
--alter table patient_form add foreign key (client_id) references client(id);


--this is for the messages between doctors and patients
drop table if exists message cascade;
create table message (
  id serial primary key,
  client_id int,
  user_id_from int,
  user_id_to int,
  patient_id_from int,
  patient_id_to int,
  message varchar(10000),
  note_assign varchar(1000),
  status char(1), --O=Open, C=Closed
  sent_dt date, --for doctor to patient messages - NEW
  pend_dt date, --to make it not appear for a few days
  read_dt TIMESTAMP WITHOUT TIME ZONE, --date patient viewed this message
  unread_notify_dt date, --alert doctor by this date if patient does not read the message
  created TIMESTAMP WITHOUT TIME ZONE,
  created_user_id int,
  updated TIMESTAMP WITHOUT TIME ZONE,
  updated_user_id int
);

create index on message using btree (client_id, patient_id_from);
create index on message using btree (client_id, patient_id_to);
create index on message using btree (client_id, user_id_from);
create index on message using btree (client_id, user_id_to);

--technical support tickets
drop table if exists support cascade;
create table support (
  id serial primary key,
  client_id int,
  subject varchar(100),
  status_id char(3), --fk to case_status
  created TIMESTAMP WITHOUT TIME ZONE,
  created_user_id int,
  updated TIMESTAMP WITHOUT TIME ZONE,
  updated_user_id int
);

create index on support using btree (client_id);

insert into support values(1, 1, 'Upload of lab gives error message file not supported', 'W', now(), 1, now(), 1);
insert into support values(2, 1, 'Make a new signup form for me so that I can use this new form', 'WC', now(), 1, now(), 1);

select setval(pg_get_serial_sequence('support', 'id'), (select max(id) from support)); --fix primary key sequence

--alter table support add foreign key (client_id) references client(id);
--alter table support add foreign key (status_id) references case_status(id);
--alter table support add foreign key (created_user_id) references user(id);
--alter table support add foreign key (updated_user_id) references user(id);

  updated TIMESTAMP WITHOUT TIME ZONE,
  updated_user_id int
);

--patients billing and payments
drop table if exists tran cascade;
create table tran (
  id serial primary key,
  dt TIMESTAMP WITHOUT TIME ZONE,
  type_id int,
  payment_method_id int,
  amount decimal,
  note varchar(1000),
  proc_id varchar(20),
  encounter_id int,
  patient_id int,
  client_id int,
  pp_status int,    --pp means payment processor such as stripe.com.  1=success, 0=declined/failed
  pp_return text,   --this is any message or data returned from the payment processor, such as bank_account_declined etc
  created TIMESTAMP WITHOUT TIME ZONE,
  created_user_id int,
  updated TIMESTAMP WITHOUT TIME ZONE,
  updated_user_id int
);
create index on tran using btree (client_id);
create index on tran using btree (patient_id);

insert into tran values (1, (now() - interval '3 day')::date, 1, null, 200.00, 'The initial visit', null, null, 1, 1, 1, null, now(), 1, now(), 1);
insert into tran values (2, (now() - interval '2 day')::date, 3, 1, -100.00, 'The first payment', null, null, 1, 1, 1, 'stripe-return-data', now(), 1, now(), 1);
insert into tran values (3, (now() - interval '1 day')::date, 3, 1, -100.00, 'The second payment', null, null, 1, 1, 1, 'stripe-return-data', now(), 1, now(), 1);

select setval(pg_get_serial_sequence('tran', 'id'), (select max(id) from tran)); --fix primary key sequence

--alter table tran add foreign key (patient_id) references patient(id);
--alter table tran add foreign key (type_id) references tran_type(id);
--alter table tran add foreign key (payment_method_id) references payment_method(id);
--alter table tran add foreign key (encounter_id) references encounter(id);
--alter table tran add foreign key (client_id) references client(id);
--alter table tran add foreign key (created_user_id) references user(id);
--alter table tran add foreign key (updated_user_id) references user(id);


--transactions with corporate
drop table if exists tranc cascade;
create table tranc (
  id serial primary key,
  dt TIMESTAMP WITHOUT TIME ZONE,      --transaction date
  type_id int,      --1=Patient Labs, 2=Doctor Fees
  payment_method_id int,
  amount decimal(7,2),
  note varchar(1000),
  patient_id int,
  client_id int,
  pp_status int,    --pp means payment processor such as stripe.com.  1=success, 0=declined/failed
  pp_return text,   --this is any message or data returned from the payment processor, such as bank_account_declined etc
  ulta_patient int, 
  ulta_order int, 
  created TIMESTAMP WITHOUT TIME ZONE
);

--The users calendar
drop table if exists user_calendar cascade;
create table user_calendar (
  id serial primary key,
  client_id int,
  user_id int,
  patient_id int,
  appointment_type_id int,
  start_dt TIMESTAMP WITHOUT TIME ZONE,
  end_dt TIMESTAMP WITHOUT TIME ZONE,
  status char(1), --R=Requested, A=Approved, D=Declined
  title varchar(100),
  notes varchar(1000),
  reschedule boolean,   --todo remove column after jira ticket done
  reschedule_id int,
  approved TIMESTAMP WITHOUT TIME ZONE,
  approved_user_id int,
  declined TIMESTAMP WITHOUT TIME ZONE,
  declined_user_id int,
  created TIMESTAMP WITHOUT TIME ZONE,
  created_user_id int,
  updated TIMESTAMP WITHOUT TIME ZONE,
  updated_user_id int
);
create index on user_calendar using btree (client_id, user_id, patient_id, start_dt);
create index on user_calendar using btree (patient_id); --patient portal, and in frontend we prevent doctors from creating a new row where patient_id + start_dt already exists

--The users availability for appointments
drop table if exists user_schedule cascade;
create table user_schedule (
  id serial primary key,
  client_id int,
  user_id int,
  start_date_time TIMESTAMP WITHOUT TIME ZONE,
  end_date_time TIMESTAMP WITHOUT TIME ZONE,
  log_tz varchar(32),
  monday boolean,
  tuesday boolean,
  wednesday boolean,
  thursday boolean,
  friday boolean,
  active boolean,
  note varchar(1000),
  created TIMESTAMP WITHOUT TIME ZONE,
  created_user_id int,
  updated TIMESTAMP WITHOUT TIME ZONE,
  updated_user_id int
);

drop table if exists client_range cascade;
create table client_range (
  id serial primary key,
  client_id int,
  marker_id int,
  seq int,                  --the first rule is 1, then 2, then 3 etc
  compare_item char(1),     --A=Age, G=Gender
  compare_operator char(2), -->, >=, <, <=, =
  compare_to char(100),     --if range_rule=Gender then M=Male, F=Female.  If range_rule=Age then any integer.
  range_low decimal(7,3),
  range_high decimal(7,3),
  created TIMESTAMP WITHOUT TIME ZONE,
  created_user_id int,
  updated TIMESTAMP WITHOUT TIME ZONE,
  updated_user_id int
);

create index on client_range using btree (client_id, marker_id, seq);


insert into client_range (client_id,marker_id,seq,compare_item,compare_operator,compare_to,range_low,range_high,created,created_user_id,updated,updated_user_id) values ( 1, 866, 1, '', '', '', 82, 88, now(), 1, now(), 1); /*Glucose*/

Create or replace procedure clientSetup(cid int, uid int)
LANGUAGE 'plpgsql'
AS $BODY$
declare count int;
declare v_id int;
declare v_client_form_id int;
declare v_user_schedule_id int;
declare v_client_range_id int;
begin

select count(*) into count
from client 
where id=cid;

if (count = 0) then
    select 'error client id does not exist in the client table';
end if;

select count(*) into count
from users 
where id=uid;

if count = 0 then
    select 'error user id does not exist in the user table';
end if;


insert into appointment_type (client_id,appointment_type,descr,length,fee,allow_patients_schedule,sort_order,active,note,created,created_user_id,updated,updated_user_id)
select  cid, appointment_type, descr, length, fee, allow_patients_schedule, sort_order, active, note, now(), uid, null, null
from appointment_type
where client_id=1;  /*client 1 is hardcoded because that is the model client*/

insert into appointment_type_user
select cid, uid, appointment_type_id, active, amount, now(), uid, null, null
from appointment_type_user
where client_id=1;

insert into client_proc
select cid, proc_id, favorite, billable, fee, null, now(), uid, null, null
from client_proc
where client_id=1;

insert into client_form (client_id,active,type,title,form,notes,created,created_user_id,updated,updated_user_id)
select  cid, active, type, title, form, notes, now(), uid, null, null
from client_form
where client_id=1
and type='S';

insert into user_schedule  (client_id,user_id,start_date_time,end_date_time,log_tz,monday,tuesday,wednesday,thursday,friday,active,note,created,created_user_id,updated,updated_user_id)
select  cid, uid, (current_date + interval '9 hour')::date, (current_date + interval '761 hour')::date, log_tz, monday, tuesday, wednesday, thursday, friday, active, null, now(), uid, null, null
from user_schedule
where client_id=1;

insert into client_range (client_id,marker_id,seq,compare_item,compare_operator,compare_to,range_low,range_high,created,created_user_id,updated,updated_user_id)
select cid, marker_id, seq, compare_item, compare_operator, compare_to, range_low, range_high, now(), uid, now(), uid
from client_range 
where client_id=1;

end;
$BODY$;


/*Test that the stored procedure works*/
call clientSetup(2, 2);


drop table if exists fda_ndc cascade;
create table fda_ndc (
    productid varchar(100),
    productndc varchar(100),
    producttypename varchar(100),
    proprietaryname varchar(1000),
    proprietarynamesuffix varchar(1000),
    nonproprietaryname varchar(1000),
    dosageformname varchar(100),
    routename varchar(100),
    startmarketingdate varchar(100),
    endmarketingdate varchar(100),
    marketingcategoryname varchar(100),
    applicationnumber varchar(100),
    labelername varchar(100),
    substancename varchar(5000),
    active_numerator_strength varchar(1000),
    active_ingred_unit varchar(1000),
    pharm_classes varchar(5000),
    deaschedule varchar(100),
    ndc_exclude_flag varchar(100),
    listing_record_certified_through varchar(100)
);


drop table if exists template cascade;
create table template (
  id serial primary key,
  client_id int,
  name varchar(100),
  content varchar(1000),
  created TIMESTAMP WITHOUT TIME ZONE,
  created_user_id int,
  updated TIMESTAMP WITHOUT TIME ZONE,
  updated_user_id int
);

create index on template using btree (client_id);

drop table if exists lab_marker cascade;
create table lab_marker (
  lab_id int,	--fk to patient_lab.id
  marker_id int,
  lab_dt TIMESTAMP WITHOUT TIME ZONE,
  line_nbr int,	--the line number of the lab
  value varchar(10),
  range_low varchar(10), --The conventional range printed on the test
  range_high varchar(10),
  unit varchar(255),
  client_id int,
  patient_id int,
  created TIMESTAMP WITHOUT TIME ZONE
);
alter table lab_marker add primary key (lab_id, marker_id);
create index on lab_marker using btree (patient_id); --patient.png
create index on lab_marker using btree (marker_id); --test.png

--alter table lab_marker add foreign key (marker_id) references marker(id);
--alter table lab_marker add foreign key (client_id) references client(id);
--alter table lab_marker add foreign key (patient_id) references patient(id);
